 lekin is baar kii sarkaar pichhali 49 dinon kii sarkaar se bhinn thi

 shiv upasna ke paanch akshar hai - "namah shivaay"
 Shiva is the controller of the universe
 sristi paanch tatwon se milakar bani he
 The five elements of creation can be controlled with these five letters
 har akshar kaa apana arth or mahatv he
 When these five letters are chanted together then creation can be controlled
 "na" akshar kaa arth or mahatv kya he?- iskaa arth nagendra se he, arthath naagon ko dhaaran karne vaale- na kaa arth nirantar shuddh rahane se bhi he- is akshar ke prayog se vyakti daso dishaao se surakshit rahata he"m" akshar kaa arth or isaki mahima kya he?- iskaa arth mandakini ko dhaaran karne se he- is akshar kaa arth mahakaal or mahadev se bhi he- nadiyon , parvaton or pushpon ko niyantrit karne ke kaaran is akshar kaa prayog hua- yah jal tatva ko niyantrit karata he"sha" akshar kaa arth or isaki mahima?- iskaa arth shiv dwaara shakti ko dhaaran karne se he- yah param kalyankari akshar mana jaataa he- is akshar se jivan main apaar sukh or shanti kii prapti hoti he"va" akshar kaa arth or isaki mahima?- iskaa sambandh shiv ke mastak ke trinetra se he- yah akshar shiv ji ke prachand swarup ko bataata he- iskaa prayog grahon nakshatron ko niyantrit karata he"ya" akshar kaa arth or isaki mahima?- is akshar kaa arth he ki , shiv ji hi aadi, anadi or anant hai- yah sampoornataa kaa akshar he- isamen shiv ko sarvavyaapak mana gaya he- is akshar kaa prayog shiv kii krupa dilaataa hapanchakshari mantra yaa panchakshari stotra kaa paath kis prakaar kalyankari hota he?- panchakshar mantra se har prakaar kii manokamana purna kii ja sakati he- isi prakaar panchakshari stotra se shiv krupa paayi ja sakati he- panchakshari stotra se man kii har tarah kii samasya dur kii ja sakati he Former President APJ Abdul Kalam said that the Unique Identification Number (UID) program launched by the government will help in combating corruption in the execution of public services

 "he said" Recently India has started the world's largest project for the identification of citizens, which will be implemented through the UID scheme

 kab milti he gracuty?• gracuty paane ke liye imploi ko kisi santhaan main lagaataar 5 saal naukari karnaa jaruri he
 • After this, gratuity is also paid for leaving the job or retiring, dying or sickness or incapable of accident
 • haalanki mrityu yaa aksham ho jane par gracuty amount die jane ke liye naukari ke 5 saal puure hona jaruri nahin he
 • In case of death, the gratuity amount will be given to his nominee, in case of non-nomination, the amount will be given to his successor
 kitne din main mil jaati he?• imploir ke liye imploi ke naukari chhodane, ritair hone, mrityu yaa uske aksham hone par 30 din ke andar gracuty die jane kaa praavdhaan he

 durgashtami or navami ke din in kanyaon ko nau devi kaa rup maanakar inkaa swaagat kiya jaataa he

 kyon or kaise kiya jaataa he kanya pujan?navaratri parv ke dauraan kanya pujan kaa bada mahatv he

 Method of Kanya Worship- Kanya are invited for banqueting and worship a day in advance
 - mukhya kanya pujan ke din idhar-udhar se kanyaon ko pakad ke laana sahi nahin hota he
 - At the entrance of the house, welcome the girls with full family flowers and show them all the nine names of Nav Durga
 - ab in kanyaon ko aaramdaayak or svachh jagah bithakar sabhi ke pairon ko doodh se bhare thaal yaa thali main rakhkar apane haathon se unke pair dhone chahie or pair chhukar ashish lenaa chahie
 - After that, apply akshat, flowers and kunkum on the forehead
 - phir maa bhagwati kaa dhyaan karke in devi rupi kanyaon ko ichha anusaar bhojan karaaen
 After the meal, give dakshina, gifts to the girls according to their ability and bless them by touching their feet again

 Just as the worship of the mother is not complete without Bhairava, in the same way it is very important to provide food to a child at the time of worshiping the girl
 yadi 9 se zyada kanya bhoj par aa rahi he to koi aapatti nahin he
 Worshiping the female form according to age- Navaratri is worshiped on all the dates one by one and on Ashtami or Navami nine girls are worshiped

 - The eight-year-old girl is called Shambhavi

 The nine-year-old girl is called Durga

 - The ten year old girl is called Subhadra
 subhadra apane bhakton ke saare manorath purna karti he
